\mapleresult
\begin{maplelatex}
\mapleinline{inert}{2d}{Pt := proc (r, t) options operator, arrow; -(diff(Y(r, t), r, t, t))/(diff(Y(r, t), r))-(diff(Y(r, t), t, t))/Y(r, t)-(diff(Y(r, t), t))*(diff(Y(r, t), r, t))/(Y(r, t)*(diff(Y(r, t), r))) end proc}{\[\displaystyle {\it Pt}\, := \,( {r,t} )\mapsto 0\]}
\end{maplelatex}
\end{maplegroup}
\begin{maplegroup}
\begin{mapleinput}
\mapleinline{active}{2d}{Anzats := Pt(r, t)-Pr(r, t)-(h-1)*r*(diff(Pr(r, t), r))/(2*h)}{\[{\it Anzats}\, := \,{\it Pt} \left( r,t \right) -\Pr \left( r,t \right) -1/2\,{\frac { \left( h-1 \right) r{\frac {\partial }{\partial r}}\Pr \left( r,t \right) }{h}}\]}
\end{mapleinput}
\mapleresult
\begin{maplelatex}

\begin{mapleinput}

\end{mapleinput}
\mapleresult
\begin{maplelatex}
\mapleinline{inert}{2d}{Anzats := -(diff(Y(r, t), t, t, r))/(diff(Y(r, t), r))+(diff(Y(r, t), t, t))/Y(r, t)-(diff(Y(r, t), t))*(diff(Y(r, t), t, r))/(Y(r, t)*(diff(Y(r, t), r)))+(diff(Y(r, t), t))^2/Y(r, t)^2-Typesetting:-delayDotProduct(beta*(2*(diff(Y(r, t), t))*(diff(Y(r, t), t, r))/(Y(r, t)*(diff(Y(r, t), r)))-2*(diff(Y(r, t), t, t))/Y(r, t)), (diff(Y(r, t), t))^2/Y(r, t)^2+2*(diff(Y(r, t), t))*(diff(Y(r, t), t, r))/(Y(r, t)*(diff(Y(r, t), r)))+Typesetting:-delayDotProduct(1/2*(-6.*(diff(Y(r, t), t, t))/Y(r, t)-3.*(diff(Y(r, t), t))^2/Y(r, t)^2), r^3/m(r, t)))}{\[\displaystyle {\it Anzats}\, := \,-{\frac {{\frac {\partial ^{3}}{\partial r\partial {t}^{2}}}Y \left( r,t \right) }{{\frac {\partial }{\partial r}}Y \left( r,t \right) }}+{\frac {{\frac {\partial ^{2}}{\partial {t}^{2}}}Y \left( r,t \right) }{Y \left( r,t \right) }}-{\frac { \left( {\frac {\partial }{\partial t}}Y \left( r,t \right)  \right) {\frac {\partial ^{2}}{\partial r\partial t}}Y \left( r,t \right) }{Y \left( r,t \right) {\frac {\partial }{\partial r}}Y \left( r,t \right) }}+{\frac { \left( {\frac {\partial }{\partial t}}Y \left( r,t \right)  \right) ^{2}}{ \left( Y \left( r,t \right)  \right) ^{2}}}\\
\mbox{}-{\it delayDotProduct} \left( \beta\, \left( 2\,{\frac { \left( {\frac {\partial }{\partial t}}Y \left( r,t \right)  \right) {\frac {\partial ^{2}}{\partial r\partial t}}Y \left( r,t \right) }{Y \left( r,t \right) {\frac {\partial }{\partial r}}Y \left( r,t \right) }}-2\,{\frac {{\frac {\partial ^{2}}{\partial {t}^{2}}}Y \left( r,t \right) }{Y \left( r,t \right) }} \right) \\

\mbox{}}{{\it \_F2} \left( t \right) }} \right\} ] \right) \]}
\end{maplelatex}

\begin{maplelatex}
\mapleinline{inert}{2d}{Pr := proc (r, t) options operator, arrow; 2*(diff(A(r, t), r))/(A(r, t)*Y(r, t)*(diff(Y(r, t), r)))-2*(diff(Y(r, t), t, t))/(Y(r, t)*A(r, t)^2)-(diff(Y(r, t), t))^2/(Y(r, t)^2*A(r, t)^2)+2*(diff(A(r, t), t))*(diff(Y(r, t), t))/(A(r, t)^3*Y(r, t)) end proc}{\[\displaystyle \Pr\, := \,( {r,t} )\mapsto 2\,{\frac {{\frac {\partial }{\partial r}}A \left( r,t \right) }{A \left( r,t \right) F \left( r \right) {\frac {\rm d}{{\rm d}r}}F \left( r \right) }}\]}
\end{maplelatex}
\end{maplegroup}

\mapleinline{inert}{2d}{Pt := proc (r, t) options operator, arrow; (diff(A(r, t), r, r))/((diff(Y(r, t), r))^2*A(r, t))+(diff(A(r, t), r))/(A(r, t)*Y(r, t)*(diff(Y(r, t), r)))-(diff(A(r, t), r))*(diff(Y(r, t), r, r))/((diff(Y(r, t), r))^3*A(r, t))-(diff(Y(r, t), r, t, t))/((diff(Y(r, t), r))*A(r, t)^2)-(diff(Y(r, t), t, t))/(Y(r, t)*A(r, t)^2)-(diff(Y(r, t), t))*(diff(Y(r, t), r, t))/(Y(r, t)*A(r, t)^2*(diff(Y(r, t), r)))+(diff(A(r, t), t))*(diff(Y(r, t), t))/(A(r, t)^3*Y(r, t))+(diff(A(r, t), t))*(diff(Y(r, t), r, t))/((diff(Y(r, t), r))*A(r, t)^3) end proc}{\[\displaystyle {\it Pt}\, := \,( {r,t} )\mapsto {\frac {{\frac {\partial ^{2}}{\partial {r}^{2}}}A \left( r,t \right) }{ \left( {\frac {\rm d}{{\rm d}r}}F \left( r \right)  \right) ^{2}A \left( r,t \right) }}+{\frac {{\frac {\partial }{\partial r}}A \left( r,t \right) }{A \left( r,t \right) F \left( r \right) {\frac {\rm d}{{\rm d}r}}F \left( r \right) }}\\
